<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.02.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Results of Operation and Financial Condition. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On November&#160;1, 2021, ON Semiconductor Corporation announced in a news release its financial performance for the third quarter ended October&#160;1, 2021 and other related material information (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Earnings Release</span></span>&#8221;). A copy of the Earnings Release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information in Item&#160;2.02 of this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</span> including Exhibit 99.1, is being furnished under Item&#160;2.02 and shall not be deemed to be &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Exchange Act</span></span>&#8221;), or otherwise subject to liability under that section, nor shall such information be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, regardless of any general incorporation language in such filing, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:18pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>onsemi reports Record Revenue and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Earnings per </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:18pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Share for Third Quarter 2021 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>PHOENIX, Ariz. &#150; Nov. 1, 2021 &#150;</B> ON Semiconductor Corporation (&#147;onsemi&#148;) (Nasdaq: ON) today announced results for
the third quarter of 2021 with the following highlights: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Record revenue of $1,742.1&nbsp;million, an increase of 32&nbsp;percent year-over-year </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">GAAP diluted earnings per share of $0.70 as compared to $0.38 in the quarter a year ago </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

$0.27 in the quarter a year ago </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

year-over-year </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

quarter-over-quarter and 800 basis points year-over-year </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Record GAAP operating margin of 22.9&nbsp;percent increased 600 basis points quarter-over-quarter and 1,390
basis point year-over-year </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

basis points quarter-over-quarter and 1,250 basis points year-over-year </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Free cash flow of $355.7&nbsp;million or 20.4&nbsp;percent of revenue </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">&#147;We delivered another quarter of record results driven by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">on-going</FONT> execution of our new strategy
with demand remaining strong for our intelligent power and sensing solutions in the automotive and industrial <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">end-markets.</FONT> We continue to execute our margin expansions plans which drove 310 basis points of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> gross margin improvement quarter-over-quarter. With a rapidly expanding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">design-win</FONT> funnel for disruptive applications such as electric vehicles, ADAS, industrial
automation, and alternative energy, coupled with ongoing transformational changes, we are making sustainable progress towards our target financial model,&#148; said Hassane <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">El-Khoury,</FONT> president and CEO of
onsemi. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Selected financial results for the quarter are shown below with comparable periods: </B></P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">*</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">Convertible Notes, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-cash</FONT> interest expense is calculated pursuant
to FASB&#146;s Accounting Standards Codification Topic 470: Debt. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">**</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">Diluted shares outstanding can vary as a result of, among other things, the actual exercise of options or
vesting of restricted stock units, the incremental dilutive shares from the Company&#146;s convertible senior subordinated notes, and the repurchase or the issuance of stock or convertible notes or the sale of treasury shares. In periods when the
quarterly average stock price per share exceeds $20.72 for the 1.625% Notes and $52.97 for the 0% Notes, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share count and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income per
share include the anti-dilutive impact of the Company&#146;s hedge transactions issued concurrently with the 1.625% Notes and the 0% Notes, respectively. At an average stock price per share between $20.72 and $30.70 for the 1.625% Notes and $52.97
and $74.34 for the 0% Notes, the hedging activity offsets the potentially dilutive effect of the 1.625% Notes and 0% Notes, respectively. In periods when the quarterly average stock price exceeds $30.70 for the 1.625% Notes, and $74.34 for the 0%
Notes, the dilutive impact of the warrants issued concurrently with such notes are included in the diluted shares outstanding. Both GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share counts are based on the Company&#146;s stock
price as of October&nbsp;1, 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">***</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">Special items may include: amortization of acquisition-related intangibles; expensing of appraised inventory
fair market value <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">step-up;</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs, purchased <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-process</FONT> research and development expenses; restructuring,
asset impairments and other, net; goodwill impairment charges; gains and losses on debt prepayment; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> interest expense; actuarial (gains) losses on pension plans and other pension benefits; and certain
other special items, as necessary. These special items are out of our control and could change significantly from period to period. As a result, we are not able to reasonably estimate and separately present the individual impact or probable
significance of these special items, and we are similarly unable to provide a reconciliation of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. The reconciliation that is unavailable would include a forward-looking income statement,
balance sheet and statement of cash flows in accordance with GAAP.&nbsp;For this reason, we use a projected range of the aggregate amount of special items in order to calculate our projected <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating
expense outlook. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

information to investors. We use these measures, together with GAAP measures, for internal managerial purposes and as a means to evaluate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT> comparisons.

additional way of viewing aspects of our operations that, when taken together with GAAP results and the reconciliations to corresponding GAAP financial measures that we also provide in our releases, provide a more complete understanding of factors

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, even if they have similar names. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:30pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>TELECONFERENCE </B></P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About onsemi </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">onsemi (Nasdaq: ON) is driving disruptive innovations to help build a better future. With a focus on automotive and industrial
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">end-markets,</FONT> the company is accelerating change in megatrends such as vehicle electrification and safety, sustainable energy grids, industrial automation, and 5G and cloud infrastructure. With a highly
differentiated and innovative product portfolio, onsemi creates intelligent power and sensing technologies that solve the world&#146;s most complex challenges and leads the way in creating a safer, cleaner, and smarter world. </P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ON SEMICONDUCTOR CORPORATION </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>RECONCILIATION OF GAAP VERSUS <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> DISCLOSURES (Continued) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(in millions, except per share and percentage data) </P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(1)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">Tax impact of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> special items
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(a-i)</FONT> is calculated using the federal statutory rate of 21% for all periods presented. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(2)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">The Company simplified its corporate structure by repatriating the economic rights of its <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-U.S.</FONT> intellectual property to the United States via domestication of certain foreign subsidiaries (the &#147;Domestication&#148;). The Domestication resulted in a benefit from recognizing certain deferred tax
assets, net of deferred tax liabilities, of $60.4&nbsp;million. Additionally, the Domestication caused the Company to reassess the full valuation allowance recorded against its U.S. state deferred tax assets. As a result, the Company released
approximately $49.9&nbsp;million of its valuation allowance recorded against its U.S. state deferred tax assets. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(3)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">The income tax adjustment primarily represents the use of the net operating loss, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> impact of not asserting indefinite reinvestment on earnings of our foreign subsidiaries, deferred tax expense not affecting taxes payable, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> expense
(benefit) related to uncertain tax positions. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain of the amounts in the above tables may not total due to rounding of individual
amounts. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total share-based compensation related to restricted stock units, stock grant awards and the employee stock purchase plan is included below: </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:14pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">To supplement the consolidated financial results prepared in accordance with GAAP, onsemi uses
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">certain&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,</FONT> which are adjusted from the most directly comparable GAAP measures to exclude items related to the amortization of intangible assets, amortization of acquisition-related
intangibles, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,&nbsp;inventory</FONT> valuation adjustments, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">purchased&nbsp;in-process&nbsp;research</FONT> and
development expenses, restructuring, asset impairments and other, net, goodwill impairment charges, gains and losses on debt <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">prepayment,&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;interest</FONT> expense, actuarial (gains) losses on pension
plans and other pension benefits, third party acquisition and divestiture related costs, tax impact of these items and certain other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> items, as necessary. Management does not consider the effects
of these items in evaluating the core operational activities of onsemi. Management uses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> internally to make strategic decisions, forecast future results and evaluate
onsemi&#146;s current performance. In addition, the Company believes that most analysts covering onsemi use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> to evaluate onsemi&#146;s performance. Given management&#146;s and
other relevant use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,</FONT> onsemi believes these measures are important to investors in understanding onsemi&#146;s current and future operating results as seen through the eyes
of management. In addition, management believes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> are useful to investors in enabling them to better assess changes in onsemi&#146;s core business across different time periods.
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">These&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> are not prepared in accordance with, and should not be considered alternatives or necessarily superior to, GAAP financial data and may be different <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">from&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> used by other companies. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Because&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures are not standardized, it may not be possible to compare these financial
measures with other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">companies&#146;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures, even if they have similar names. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Revenue </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> revenue allows
management to evaluate, among other things, the revenue from the Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent of special items. In addition,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-</FONT> GAAP revenue is an important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the
business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future results. Management presents this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate
the Company&#146;s revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of onsemi&#146;s core businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Gross</FONT> Profit and Gross Margin </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;gross</FONT> profit and gross margin allows management to evaluate, among other things, the gross margin and gross profit of the Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different
reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT> including, generally speaking, expensing of appraised inventory fair market
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up</FONT> and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs. In addition, it is an important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and
reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">this&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate our revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of revenue of onsemi&#146;s core businesses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Operating</FONT> Income and&nbsp;Operating Margin </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;operating</FONT> income and operating margin allows management to evaluate,
among other things, the operating margin and operating income of the Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT>
including, generally speaking, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs,&nbsp;amortization and impairments of
intangible assets, third party acquisition and divestiture related costs, restructuring charges and certain other special items as necessary. In addition, it is an important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and
incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">this&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate the Company&#146;s revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of onsemi&#146;s core businesses.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Net</FONT> Income Attributable to ON Semiconductor Corporation and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Diluted Earnings Per Share </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;net</FONT> income attributable to onsemi and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per share allows management to evaluate the operating results of onsemi&#146;s core
businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT> including, generally, the amortization and impairments of intangible assets, expensing of
appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs, restructuring, gains and losses on debt
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">prepayment,&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;interest</FONT> expense, actuarial (gains) losses on pension plans and other pension benefits, third party acquisition and divestiture related costs, tax indemnification by third
parties, tax impact of these items and other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> MEASURES (Continued) </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">adjustments and certain other special items, as necessary. In addition, these items are
important components of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process, as they are used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing
budgets, setting targets and forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures to enable investors and analysts to understand the results of operations of
onsemi&#146;s core businesses and, to the extent comparable, to compare our results of operations on a more consistent basis against those of other companies in our industry. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Free Cash Flow </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of free cash
flow allows management to evaluate, among other things, the ability of the Company to make interest or principal payments on its debt. Free cash flow is defined as the difference between cash flow from operating activities and capital expenditures
disclosed under investing activities in the consolidated statement of cash flows. Free cash flow is not an alternate to cash flow from operating activities as a measure of liquidity. It is an important component of management&#146;s internal
performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future results.
Management presents this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate our revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of onsemi&#146;s core businesses.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Diluted Share Count </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share count allows management to evaluate, among other things, the
potential dilution due to the outstanding stock options and restricted stock units excluding the dilution from the convertible notes that is covered by hedging activity up to a certain threshold. In periods when the quarterly average stock price per
share exceeds $20.72, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> share count&nbsp;includes the anti-dilutive impact of the Company&#146;s hedge transactions issued concurrently with the 1.625% convertible notes. As such,
at an average stock price per share between $20.72 and $30.70, the hedging activity offsets the potentially dilutive effect of the 1.625% convertible notes. In periods when the quarterly average stock price per share exceeds $52.97, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> share count&nbsp;includes the anti-dilutive impact of the Company&#146;s hedge transactions issued concurrently with the 0% convertible notes. As such, at an average stock price per
share between $52.97 and $74.34, the hedging activity offsets the potentially dilutive effect of the 0% convertible notes. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>

</DIV></Center>
